   4: def get_label_from_ID(length, y_allowed, ID):
   5:     parsed = ID.replace('ant_data__', '')
   6: 
   7:     index_value = 1
   8:     
   9:     if y_allowed:
  10:         index_value = 2
  11: 
  12:     states = np.empty((length, index_value), dtype=float)

  16: 
  17:         first = re.sub(r'_.*', '', vec_string)
  18: 
  19:         if y_allowed:
  20:             states[i][0] = int(first)
  21: 
  22:         first += '_'
  23:         second = re.sub(first, '', vec_string)

  25:             states[i][1] = int(second)
  26:         else:
  27:             states[i][0] = int(second)
  28:             
  29:

  31:             remove_vec = vec_string + "__"
  32:             parsed = re.sub(remove_vec, '', parsed)
  33: 
  34:     return np.squeeze(states)

   1: def keras_fmin_fnct(space):
   2: 
   3: 
   4:     def not_quite_linear(x):
   5:         return K.tanh(x / 5.0) * 5.0
   6: 
   7:     def linear_bound_above_abs_1(x):
   8:         return K.switch(K.less(not_quite_linear(x), 0), x - 1, x + 1)
   9:     
  10:     get_custom_objects().update({'linear_bound_above_abs_1': Activation(linear_bound_above_abs_1)})
  11:     get_custom_objects().update({'not_quite_linear': Activation(not_quite_linear)})
  12:     model = Sequential()
  13:     model.add(torus_transform_layer((11,11),input_shape=(51,51,1)))
  14:     model.add(Convolution2D(32, (11, 11), activation='not_quite_linear'))
  15:     
  16:     model.add(torus_transform_layer((11,11)))
  17:     model.add(Convolution2D(32, (11, 11), activation='not_quite_linear'))
  18:     model.add(MaxPooling2D((2,2), strides=(2,2)))
  19: 
  20:     model.add(torus_transform_layer((5,5)))
  21:     model.add(Convolution2D(32, (5, 5), activation='not_quite_linear'))
  22:     model.add(MaxPooling2D((2,2), strides=(2,2)))
  23:

  27:

  29:     model.add(Convolution2D(64, (3, 3), activation='not_quite_linear'))

  31:

  46:     model.add(Dense(length, activation=linear_bound_above_abs_1))
